return(function(...)local C,e,E=table,string,bit local D,K,H,M,B,N,f,o,I,L,F=e.byte,e.char,e.sub,C.concat,C.insert,math.ldexp,getfenv and getfenv()or _ENV,setmetatable,select,unpack or
